# Parity Gaps — ranked by gameplay impact

_Generated 2026-06-22. 1363 features with gaps, highest-impact first._

Score weights logic & liveness highest, then values/timing, then presentation/audio, scaled by category (core gameplay > niche entities). Intended divergences excluded.

| # | score | unit | feature | worst | gaps |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | 28.5 | `weapon-machinegun` | `machinegun.audio.impact_ricochet` | logic:missing | Firing the MachineGun at a wall plays the impact PARTICLE (MACHINEGUN_IMPACT) but no ricochet PING — the random ric1/ric2/ric3 sound from Base's wr_impacteffect is never played. SoundSystem.Ric()/PlayRic() (SoundSystem.cs:65/195) are registered but have no live caller; FireOne emits the impact effect without a ric sound. |
| 2 | 28.5 | `weapon-rifle` | `rifle.reload` | logic:missing | The rifle never reloads: FireBullets drains the pool (rifle.ammo.decrease) so clip_load never decrements (it's seeded to 80 by the driver and stays there), the forced-reload branch at the top of wr_think is absent, the secondary `reload` flag is ignored, and CheckAmmoPrimary/Secondary omit the weapon_load[] clip term that QC wr_checkammo1/2 OR in. No SND_RELOAD, no 2s downtime, no 80-round cap — the rifle's defining reload cadence is absent on the live path. |
| 3 | 27.0 | `assault` | `assault.mapobject.assault_wall` | logic:missing | func_assault_wall edicts are consumed with no behavior: the wall that should hide (model='' + SOLID_NOT) once its objective is destroyed and reappear otherwise does neither, so a path that QC opens by destroying an objective stays blocked (or vice versa). |
| 4 | 27.0 | `weapon-crylink` | `crylink.linkjoin.joinexplode_bonus` | logic:missing | LinkJoin never spawns the meeting-time linkjoineffect think (crylink.qc:529-534), so the convergence count (>=2 spikes near the meeting point) and the joinexplode RadiusDamage are never evaluated.; EFFECT_CRYLINK_JOINEXPLODE is never emitted at the convergence point (the sparkle when a held primary burst meets on release is missing). The port DOES emit CRYLINK_JOINEXPLODE — but from LinkExplode (a different trigger Base never uses for it).; joinexplode bonus damage/edge/radius/force scaled by (n/shots) is absent; moot at stock balance (all 0) but the feature is fully unimplemented.; The joinexplode cvars (primary_joinexplode + *_damage/edge/radius/force) are not even read in Configure() — there is no PrimaryJoinExplode field; only PrimaryLinkExplode (a different cvar) exists. |
| 5 | 26.7 | `weapon-tuba` | `weapon-tuba.reload.instrument_cycle` | liveness:dead | Pressing reload does nothing for the tuba: WeaponImpulses.ReloadHandle calls Weapon.WrReload (the generic gate), which early-returns because Tuba lacks WeaponFlags.Reloadable. Tuba.Reload (the real instrument-cycle override) is a plain public method with ZERO callers (verified by grep; only binary DLLs and an unrelated Menu DataSource.Reload match).; Player can never switch to Accordion or Klein Bottle: view model, sound set and obituary are permanently Tuba.; Even if wired, Tuba.Reload is not faithful: it omits the WS_READY guard, sets no weaponname, plays misc/teleport.wav instead of Send_Effect(EFFECT_TELEPORT), and skips the WS_INUSE/WFRAME_RELOAD 0.5s animation lock. |
| 6 | 24.45 | `weapon-tuba` | `weapon-tuba.audio.note_sound` | logic:missing | The single per-blast Sound.Play targets 'weapons/tuba_loopnote.wav', which does NOT exist in port data — the real samples are per-pitch tuba_loopnote0/6/12/18/24/-6/-12/-18 (+ tuba1_*/tuba2_* per instrument), all .ogg. The base unpitched filename has no '0'/number suffix, so the lookup matches nothing and almost certainly plays silence (the host resolver maps .wav->.ogg but cannot invent a missing base name). Not even a working static placeholder.; No sustained note: even if the asset existed, the port fires one static sample per blast tick (~every 0.05s) rather than a held, pitched loop that fades on release.; Pitch is ignored (no per-note sample selection, no sound7 pitch step / two-sample crossfade).; No fade-out (cl_tuba_fadetime), no client volume/attenuation cvars, no per-listener distance attenuation.; No ENT_CLIENT_TUBANOTE networking; remote players' tuba notes are not driven by the dedicated note entity. |

(CENTER_ALONE) print to the last survivor of a team (ca_LastPlayerForTeam_Notify not ported).; The round-win announcer cue never plays. |

Roles never swap; the faster-destroyer overall winner is never decided.; The 5s AS_ROUND_DELAY freeze + ReadyRestart_force map reset + bprint('Starting second round...') are not implemented.; Round 2's timelimit (= round 1 destruction time) is recorded as FirstRoundDestroyTime but never applied to any clock. |
